<H>{@sAraLA mahAbhArata@}

<H>{@gaNezaGka bandanA@}

<P>jay1a tu amrutAkSa jay1a tu gaNapati

<P>praLay1a uddhAraNa nAtha bizwambhara mUrati | 1 |

<P>parazu pAza aMku za amruta laDu bhojI

<P>kaNay1a sudhArasa haraSeNa bhmaMji | 2 |

<P>bighna nibArana nAtha bighnaMka airi

<P>prasanne paramabandhu jay1a tu digAmbarI | 3 |

<P>praLay1a uddhAraNa tu nAtha bizwabAsI

<P>drazane sabongsiddhi apAda dukha dhwaMsi | 4 |

<P>y1e zarIraku ApAda ye aTai mahabighna

<P>bighnarAja bihune nAhiMnA mana Ana | 5 |

<P>nAzagalA prANIki krutAnteka diai zAsti

<P>se krutAntaka dhwaMsanaku abhay1e gaNapati | 6 |

<P>maraNakai mULa ye aTai yeuM bighna mAna

<P>teNukari yamara darpa gaMjilu gajAnana | 7 |

<P>yamakai gaMjilu nAtha ye saMsAra dukha dekhi

<P>nAzita buddhi kalu tohora day1A ye upekhi | 8 |

<P1>5|2 bighna ban~chi na pArile hoi nAzapAna | (cha, ka)

[MBO-03(1)-002]

<P>bikaLe nAzakara paLAilA gopye

<P>bibare pazilA yAiM indUra sarUpe | 9 |

<P>kALaphAsi lagAi tAku kilusi bandhana

<P>trAseNa zaraNa totye pazilA janturANa | 10 |

<P>zaraNa uddhAraNa tu aTu ho bizubAsI

<P>zaraNa rakSAkalu deba tAhi prANe na nAzi | 11 |

<P>bhagatajana matsaLa tu deba gajAnana

<P>se yama indUrakai deba kalusi bAhAna | 12 |

<P>mahAbhArA rUpa tora kahita ke pAri

<P>yama se indUra rUpe bAhAna tohori | 13 |

<P>bighnamAnaMka rAjA rAjye aTe mULa

<P>ati duSTapaNa dekhi tAku thoilu jAnutaLa | 14 |

<P>mahamanda AchArI se aTai deba jarA

<P>saMsAra nAzakalA se amrutAkSa asurA | 15 |

<P>yama boilA deba mote kopakalu

<P>jarA se baDa manda tu y1ehAku rakhilu | 16 |

<P>prANIku nAza karibAku jwara mohora daNDa

<P>zate zate roga y1e aTai ta durddaNDa | 17 |

<P>prathama senApati se aTai mohori

<P>y1ehAkuiM gheni se muM prANIMkara darpa hari | 18 |

<P>yamara bacane deba dhailu duSTa jarA

<P>padeNa mADilu kaThAu cUraNa mahAbhArA | 19 |

<P>y1e kaLikAle hoanTa aneka anIti

<P>jANiNa sabonggyaMnAtha ye sabunti nibartti | 20 |

<P1>15|2 mandara samAna aTe jarAra zarIra
<>saMsAra nAzakalA se duSTa asura || (Tha)

<P1>19| debongkara bacane deba dhailu duSTa jarA
<>pAde maradilu deba kaNay1a giri bhArA || (cha)

[MBO-03(1)-004]

<P>mana bacana karttabya ye bAn~cchA saMkalpe

<P>taba drazane nAtha dhwaMsa na honti cira pApe | 35 |

<P>nirAlamba puruSa bacane sabongkalpi

<P>kaLikALa dhwaMsi nAtha rakSaNa sabongtapI | 36 |

<P>zrI tuLusAra ballabha caraNa dhari zire

<P>sabongpApa haru nAtha binAy1aka abatare | 37 |

<P>day1AkaiM kAraNa tu kAraNakaiM sAdhu

<P>mama pAtaka bidhwaMsantA jagata jana bandhu | 38 |

<P>muhiMta mUrkha deba aTai agyAna

<P>taba lay1e gyAna mote hoibA prasanna | 39 |

<P>zrI bighnarAjaMka caraNe zatesahasra daNDa praNamya

<P>teNukari zUdramuni sAroLA dAs mora nAma | 40 |

<P>jaGkherapura bAsI ye abhay1e aparNNA

<P>se mohora zarIraku aTai bajrasenahA | 41 |

<P>tahiM mora citta ye thAu sabong kALe | 45 |

[MBO-03(1)-005]

<H>{@baLarAmaGka nikagare zrIkruSNaGkara yamapura darzana
<>barNNana o nAradaGkaThAru yudhiSThi raGkara
<>pANDu rAjAGka durddazA zrabaNa@}

<P>bilaMka dezara rAjA baibasuta manu

<P>pAdya arghya dei pUjAkalA se ghaTaruSira tanu | 1 |

<P>basana kuNDaLa ratnamALa dhUpadIpa naibidya

<P>pan~chulakSa hiraNya deiNa pUjilA muniMka padmapAda | 2 |

<P>bho brahmaruSi taba caraNe mora sebA

<P>y1e sabhApabong kathA mote bizeSi kahibA | 3 |

<P>boila ye Adipabonge paNDurAjA kay1e brahmahatyA

<P>kemante paNDu brahmahatyA dhwaMsana galA brahmabettA | 4 |

<P>y1ehA mahatamA mote kahibA agastiy1e

<P>bongze brahmahatyA thile kemante nibhrAnti hoiba munihe | 5 |

<P>badanti agasti kaLapi mahatamA

<P>pratakSe nArAy1aNa se anadi siddhabrahmA | 6 |

<P>tuLamAsa zukaLa pakSa dazamI gurubAra

<P>dhaniSThA nAme nakSatra aTai se dinara | 7 |

<P>taitiLa nAme karaNa bruddhi nAme yoga

<P>tuLa saMkarAntiki pAn~chadina bhoga | 8 |

<P>bijay1e nArAy1aNa deba nILAmbare

<P>kAmapALe pucchAkale gobindaMka chAmure | 9 |

<P>bhAbeNa kathAy1e pucchA kale debarAje

<P>yamara saMjIbanI puraku hari karithilu bije | 10 |

<P>guru pan~chaputranta kaluTi kemanta

<P>khoji pAilunA ho kaha deba jagabhUta | 11 |

<P1>9| dine nArAy1aNa bije dwArikA sudharmA sabhAre
<>kAmapALa puccchAkale gobinda sannidhare || (tha)

[MBO-03(1)-006]

<P>badanti jagannAthe zuNimA deba kAmapAje

<P>yamara sabhAku muM gali yetebeLe | 12 |

<P>dekhina aneka pApI hoile mukata

<P>nAzakara aneka zAsti ye deuthile manuSyanta | 13 |

<P>mohor adrazane aneka pApIjane

<P>pAile parama gati ye basile swargasthAne | 14 |

<P>guruMka pan~chaputra muM yAuthili loDi

<P>yamaNe mAruthile aneka pApIMki pApIMki bihaDi | 15 |

<P>bahuta pAtekImAne narkakuNDe thile paDi | 16 |

<P>mama drazane kari pAile mokSagati

<P>dekhiNa trAsilA krutAntaka Adhipati | 17 |

<P>subarNNa thALire dubongAkSata argya gheni

<P>mama pAda pUjAkalA ye nAtha saMjIbanI | 18 |

<P>aneka trAseNa se bahuta binay1e

<P>praNapatya kari se basAilA sabhAy1e | 19 |

<P>chAmure karapatra yoDiNa nAzakara

<P>nistarili swAmI Aja aneka bhAgya mohora | 20 |

<P>y1e saMjIbanI pure paDilA y1e tohora pAdaraja

<P>bahuta aprAdhi pApI trAhikalu bebarAja | 21 |

<P>mote anugraha ki taba kAryya arthe

<P>nAzara pUraku swAmI he bijay1e ki nimante | 22 |

<P>bolanti kezaba tumbhe zaNa ho jantupati

<P>aLapa kAryye Ambhe ailu tohora y1ethi | 23 |

<P1>15|2 yamagaNe mAruthile ye aneka zAsti kari | (tha, Ga, jha, gha, Dha)

[MBO-03(1)-007]

<P>zAntipanI paNDA ye Ambhara bydyAguru

<P>tAhAMkara putraku tu kimpAi hAde haru | 24 |

<P>AmbhaMku dakSiNA se mAgile hAde guru

<P>gyAna pAile se Ambhara zAsra paRhu | 25 |

<P>mruta pan~chuputra mAgile bahuta kaTALe

<P>tada arthe ailuM tora saMjIbanI maNDaLe | 26 |

<P>tAhAnta dile Ambhanti bidyA hoiba prApata | 27 |

[MBO-03(1)-010]

<P>yathArtha hoiNa yebe tohora cittare zuddha thAntA

<P>karapatra yoDiNa jagannAthe boile

<P>Izwara debatA pUbonge brahmahatyA kale | 58 |

<P>sehi aneka kaSThore pArakari nuArile

[MBO-03(1)-083]
